create table CLOIDATIN
(

	RSD_DISUSE_YN varchar(1) null comment '잔여폐기여부',
	REC_HIST_SN decimal(22) null comment '기록이력일련번호',
	ORDR_DIRECT_DT varchar(8) null comment '처방지시일자',
	ORDR_CANCEL_CD varchar(1) null comment '처방취소코드',
	REC_ORDR_SHAP_CD varchar(4) null comment '기록처방형태코드',
	ORDR_CD varchar(11) null comment '처방코드',
	ORDR_CNTE varchar(4000) null comment '처방내용',
	DOSAGE decimal(15,4) null comment '투여량',
	CNTNT_MSR_NM varchar(400) null comment '함량단위명',
	MDCT_REC_AOM_MTH_CD varchar(3) null comment '투약기록투여방법코드',

	TOT_PFORM_QT decimal(20,9) null comment '총수행용량',
	TOT_PFORM_CNT decimal null comment '총수행횟수',
	PFORM_RTUN_QT decimal(15,9) null comment '수행반납용량',
	ORDR_PFORM_LOC_CD varchar(5) null comment '처방수행장소코드',
	REAL_ORDR_LOC_USE_CD varchar(5) null comment '실처방장소사용코드',
	MDCT_REC_OVLAP_YN varchar(1) null comment '투약기록중복여부',
	PFORM_ORDR_OVLAP_YN varchar(1) null comment '수행처방중복여부',
	ORDR_STORG_YN varchar(1) null comment '처방저장여부',
	MDCT_REC_YN varchar(1) null comment '투약기록여부',
	ORDR_CHOIC_YN varchar(1) null comment '처방선택여부',
	MEDI_MIX_YN varchar(1) null comment '의약품혼합여부',
	CNTI_INFS_MEDI_PFORM_POSBL_YN varchar(1) null comment '지속주입의약품수행가능여부',
	UPR_ORDR_PFORM_NO varchar(32) null comment '상위처방수행번호',
	ORDR_DEL_YN varchar(1) null comment '처방삭제여부',
	RCIV_DT varchar(8) null comment '수납일자',
	RCIV_TM varchar(6) null comment '수납시각',
	ORDR_PFORM_ENTR_PROGRM_CD varchar(3) null comment '처방수행입력프로그램코드',
	VALD_YN varchar(1) null comment '유효여부',
	VACCIN_LOT_NO varchar(30) null comment '예방접종LOT번호',
	IR_WAIT_NO varchar(15) null comment '주사실대기번호',
	STAT_EX_YN varchar(1) null comment '통계제외여부',
	ORDR_OCCUR_CLSF_CD varchar(1) null comment '처방발생분류코드',
	PFORM_PNTM_AGE_VAL decimal null comment '수행시점나이값',

	SRC_LOAD_DTM datetime null comment '원천적재일시',
	ETL_LOAD_DTM datetime null comment 'ETL적재일시',
	primary key (ORDR_PFORM_NO, DRAWUP_SN, DRAWUP_HIST_SN, PFORM_DT, MTRL_DIV_NM)
)
comment '통합처방수행정보상세'
;
